# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:

    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.

    shared_elements = []

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the common elements from the given two lists.
def common_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    common_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements


# Write a function to find the common elements from the given two lists.
def common_elements_2(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    common_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

    common_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements


# Write a function to find the common elements from the given two lists.
def common_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    common_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements

def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements


# Write a function to find the common elements from the given two lists.

            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements

# Write a function to find the shared elements from the given two lists.
def similar_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    shared_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            shared_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return shared_elements


# Write a function to find the common elements from the given two lists.
def common_elements(test_tup1, test_tup2):
    common_elements = []
    for i in range(len(test_tup1)):
        if test_tup1[i] in test_tup2:
            common_elements.append(test_tup1[i])
    return common_elements
